/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetUrl]    Script Date: 06/18/2018 16:34:58 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetUrl]
  @FilesId int,
  @Url nvarchar(100) output
AS
BEGIN
select @Url=NavigateUrl 
from tbTree 
where Files_Id=@FilesId
END
GO

) ON [PRIMARY]
